рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреА рейрез рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБ рд╢реНрд░реА-рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛рдирдиреНрджрдШрдиреЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирд╛ #резрейрелрей

Observed on ┼Ъukla-Dv─Бda┼Ы─л tithi of ─Ас╣г─Бс╕Нhaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3769 (kali era).
Born on the banks of river Garuс╕Нa (Kaс╕Нilam in Tamil) in the Draviс╕Нa de┼Ыa (South India), as the son of Anant─Бrya, He was called Jyeс╣гс╣нarudra (before initiation). Having become the disciple of ┼Ъr─л Bodhendr─Бc─Бrya, He held with sincerity the responsibility of Preceptor-ship of the earth; worshipped by King Lalit─Бditya of Kashmir who conquered all rival kings on earth ┼Ъr─л Brahm─Бnandaghana attained liberation on dv─Бda┼Ы─л(twelfth day) of the bright fortnight of Jyeс╣гс╣нa in the year Prabhava. Well-versed in the six system of philosophy and adored/worshipped by the well-known poet Bhavabh┼лti and Kashmir monarch Lalit─Бditya, this preceptor adorned the P─лс╣нha for thirteen years and attained liberation in K─Б├▒ci itself.

Born of Mah─Бbal─л┼Ыvare┼Ыvara by name Mahe┼Ыvara, the other Sure┼Ыvara, adhering to austerities obtained the responsibility of governing the K─Б├▒ci K─Бmakoс╣нi P─лс╣нha of the preceptor of the entire earth, He, the pure reached his imperishable state in the month of ─Ас╣г─Бс╕Нha of the year Akс╣гaya.

рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреА рейрео рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБ рд╢реНрд░реА-рдЕрднрд┐рдирд╡рд╢рдЩреНрдХрд░реЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирд╛ #резрезреорез

Observed on Am─Бv─Бsy─Б tithi of ─Ас╣г─Бс╕Нhaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3941 (kali era).
This preceptor was the son of Vi┼Ыvajit of Cidambaram through vi┼Ыiс╣гс╣н─Б; like the Sun who dispels the dense darkness veiling his presence, He was born on the tenth day of the bright fortnight in the month of Vai┼Ы─Бkha in the year Vibhava twelve months after his fatherтАЩs demise. One who was abandoned as a child in the midst of a forest by his mother herself without any possible solution to her deplorable plight, viz., widowhood, lack of shelter, servitude, insult of relatives fear of slander etc. Who, on crying at a distance was taken by the wife of Vy─Бghrap─Бda, to her home and was compassionately breastfed by her after informing her husband. The sage initiated him and imparted the ─Бtmavidy─Б. Then, the adept in self control/ascetic principles, having completed studies, well-versed in scriptures, having received the grace bestowed by the Universal Preceptor (┼Ъr─л ┼Ъaс╣Еkara) who manifested of his will before (him), and having received the mighty sacred sandals (of ┼Ъr─л ┼Ъaс╣Еkara) offered by Padmap─Бda appearing by the side of ┼Ъr─л ┼Ъaс╣Еkara, He (the Dh─лra┼Ыaс╣Еkara) stayed in Tilvaraс╣Зya. The Universal Preceptor having adorned the seat of K─БmaP─лс╣нha, He wandered through the earth triumphant of having wiped off the arrogance of the adherents/scholars of rival schools in eight quarters (of the earth) and established the doctrine of Advaita. He ┼Ъaс╣Еkarendra, having conquered easily the Kashmiri scholars Girodbhaс╣нс╣нa and others, ascended the Sarvaj├▒aP─лс╣нha in Kashmir and though being followed by disciples to the ─Аtreya caves (in the Himalayas), disappeared alive in the embodied form itself. Thus, the preceptor sage spreading/showering the tenets of Advaya on this sacred earth for fifty-two years and with a desire to spread this noble path in the other world, He disappeared on the new moon day in the month of ─Ас╣г─Бс╕Нha of the Uttarayaс╣Зa in the year Siddh─Бrthi of Kali era 3914. The sage Saccidvil─Бsa became the preceptor. This preceptor is tur─лyat─лta-┼Ъaс╣Еkara. Some scholars mistake him to be ┼Ъr─л ┼Ъaс╣Еkara Bhagavadp─Бda and compile biography with inconsistencies.

Observed on Am─Бv─Бsy─Б tithi of ─Ас╣г─Бс╕Нhaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 4199 (kali era).
He, Soma, initiated with the title Bodhendra by the preceptor Para┼Ыivendra adorned the P─лс╣нha and visiting countries in the palanquin exquisitely decked with gems offered by Bhoja, the king of Dh─Бr─Б, inculcating faith in the principles of Advaita in the minds of those who venerated him on the path safeguarded the Maс╣нha from the invaders (mlechas) with the help of the minister of the Kashmiri King Kala┼Ыa. Having stayed in the P─лс╣нha for thirty-seven years, He reached the Supreme Abode at Aruс╣З─Бcala on the New moon day of the month ─Ас╣г─Бс╕Нha in the year ─В┼Ыvara. This preceptor Bodhendra, also known as S─Бnandr─Бnanda, was honoured for poetical excellence by KingsтАФBhoja, Kala┼Ыe┼Ыvara and others and was intent on travelling through the earth.

Observed on day 23 of July (gregorian) month. Julian date was converted to Gregorian in this reckoning. The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 1660 (gregorian era).
AshADha k1 bAji prabhu deshpANDe leading ~300 men died holding back Adil-shAhi african general siddi masud’s 10k soldiers in a narrow pass while shivAji leading his 300 escaped to vishAlgad fort (having earlier let his barber take his place while escaping from another beseiged fort) and announced his safe arrival with a cannon-fire. PS: vishAlgad was already under siege by Bijapuri sardars Suryarao Surve and Jaswantrao Dalvi. it’s a thrilling tale, akin to tale of the spartans holding back the persians at the narrow pass at Thermopylae.

┼Ъivar─Бmakс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, son of Parame┼Ыvara on the banks of river Pamp─Б, devoted to Sad─Б┼Ыiva, having got initiation into asceticism from him, devoid of any attachment indeed, He remained at the abode of goddess K─Бm─Бkс╣г─л. This senior preceptor, courageous, reached the space that is beyond the physical body, on the tenth day of the bright fortnight of the ┼Ъravaс╣Зa month in the year P─Бrthiva of the ┼Ъaka era 1508 (D┼лra ┼Ъaka). According to scholars, this preceptor was the master of Sad─Б┼Ыivabrahmendra and attained siddhi in ┼Ъvet─Бraс╣Зyam.

Son of ┼Ъr─лpati, known as Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa before initiation, the great sage P┼лrс╣Зabodhendra, merged in Brahman on the Ek─Бda┼Ыi (eleventh) day of the bright fortnight of the month ┼Ъravaс╣Зa in the year ─В┼Ыvara. His preceptorship was for seventeen years.
